Start of set
Set #1 Toss-ups

1.	Who sought out the disciples at Tyre?
A.	Paul and his companions (21:4)
2.	Who sent Timothy and Erastus to Macedonia?
A.	Paul (19:22)
3.	What was the Ethiopian eunuch reading?
A.	The book ()of Isaiah the prophet (8:28)
4.	When did the men throw the ship’s tackle overboard with their own hands?
A.	On the third day (27:19)
5.	Whom did the Spirit tell to have no hesitation about going with the three men?
A.	Peter (11:12)
6.	Who did not intend to bring any charge against his own people?
A.	Paul (28:19)
7.	What did Stephen do among the people?
A.	Performed great wonders and signs (6:8)
8.	To whom did the voice speak a second time?
A.	Peter (10:15)
9.	Who went down to Attalia when they had preached the word in Perga?
A.	Paul and Barnabas (14:25)
10.	Who are telling you the way to be saved?
A.	These men (16:17)
11.	In what did Judas the Galilean lead a band of people?
A.	Revolt (5:37)
12.	Who does not have silver or gold?
A.	Peter (3:6)
13.	What were the apostles when the day of Pentecost came?
A.	All together in one place (2:1)
14.	Who knelt down and prayed with all of them?
A.	Paul (20:36)
15.	Of what was Judas one?
A.	The apostles’ number (1:17)
16.	What is another word for "anointed one"?
A.	Messiah or Christ (4:26)
17.	What is heaven?
A.	The Lord’s throne (7:49)
18.	What has been sent to the children of Abraham, and you God-fearing Gentiles?
A.	This message of salvation (13:26)
19.	When did Tertullus present his case before Felix?
A.	When Paul was called in (24:2)
20.	To whom did Saul go?
A.	The high priest (9:1)
21.	When was Herod wearing his royal robes?
A.	On the appointed day (12:21)
22.	With whom did some of the teachers of the law who were Pharisees find nothing wrong?
A.	This man [OR Paul] (23:9)
23.	Who even hunted the Lord’s people down in foreign cities to persecute them?
A.	Paul (26:11)
24.	What will the Lord rebuild?
A.	David’s fallen tent [OR its ruins] (15:16)
25.	Who made Jason and the others post bond and let them go?
A.	The city officials (17:9)
26.	Who traveled from place to place throughout the region of Galatia and Phrygia, strengthening all the disciples?
A.	Paul (18:23)
27.	Who became very quiet?
A.	The crowd (22:2)
28.	Who brought the tabernacle with them when they took the land from the nations God drove out before them?
A.	Our ancestors under Joshua (7:45)
29.	What did Philip hear the man reading?
A.	Isaiah the prophet (8:30)
30.	With what did the believers eat together?
A.	With glad and sincere hearts (2:46)
31.	For whom was it against the law to visit a Gentile?
A.	A Jew (10:28)
32.	To whom did the centurion take the young man?
A.	The commander (23:18)
33.	Who came in about three hours later, not knowing what had happened?
A.	Ananias’ wife (5:7)
34.	Through whom did God do extraordinary miracles?
A.	Paul (19:11)
35.	To whom had the elders written their decision that they should abstain from food sacrificed to idols, from blood, from the meat of strangled animals and from sexual immorality?
A.	The Gentile believers (21:25)
36.	To whom did James say the believers should write?
A.	The Gentiles (15:20)
37.	Where did the chief priests and the Jewish leaders appear before Festus and present the charges against Paul?
A.	Jerusalem (25:1-2)
38.	From where did a light suddenly flash around Saul?
A.	Heaven (9:3)
39.	When did Paul send for the disciples?
A.	When the uproar had ended (20:1)
40.	Who was with Barnabas and Saul as their helper?
A.	John (13:5)
41.	Who vigorously refuted his Jewish opponents in public debate, proving from the Scriptures that Jesus was the Messiah?
A.	Apollos (18:28)
42.	Who was a member of the Areopagus?
A.	Dionysius (17:34)
43.	What did the magistrates request Paul and Silas to do?
A.	Leave the city (16:39)
44.	To whom did Paul say, "Brothers and fathers, listen now to my defense."?
A.	The crowd (21:40-22:1)
45.	Who were brought before the rulers, the elders and the teachers of the law?
A.	Peter and John (4:7)
46.	What would Felix be able to learn by examining Paul himself?
A.	The truth about Paul (24:8)
47.	When did the men begin to throw the cargo overboard?
A.	The next day (27:18)
48.	To what was Paul not disobedient?
A.	The vision from heaven (26:19)
49.	According to Acts chapter 7: verse 12, what was there in Egypt?
A.	Grain (7:12)
50.	Who talked and debated with the Hellenistic Jews?
A.	Saul (9:29)
51.	What is called the Northeaster?
A.	A wind of hurricane force (27:14)
52.	According to Acts chapter 28: verse 20, with what was Paul bound?
A.	This chain (28:20)
53.	Through whom is the forgiveness of sins proclaimed to you?
A.	Jesus (13:38)
54.	Who have been informed that Paul teaches all the Jews who live among the Gentiles to turn away from Moses, telling them not to circumcise their children or live according to their customs?
A.	The Jews (21:21)
55.	Where did Agabus predict that a severe famine would spread?
A.	Over the entire Roman world (11:28)
56.	To whom did Paul make his appeal?
A.	The Emperor (25:25)
57.	Onto whom did the man who had been lame from birth hold?
A.	Peter and John (3:11)
58.	Who said, "For it is written in the book of Psalms, 'May his place be deserted; let there be no one to dwell in it,' and, 'May another take his place of leadership.'"?
A.	Peter (1:20)
59.	What will God show on the earth below?
A.	Signs (2:19)
60.	When did it belong to Ananias?
A.	Before it was sold (5:4)
61.	How was he led to the slaughter?
A.	Like a sheep (8:32)
62.	From where did the great Artemis’ image fall?
A.	Heaven (19:35)
63.	Who heard the message?
A.	Many (4:4)
64.	To whom did Paul and Silas speak the word of the Lord?
A.	The jailer and all the others in his house (16:32)
65.	To where did Peter see something like a large sheet being let down by its four corners?
A.	Earth (10:11)
66.	Who was no ordinary child?
A.	Moses (7:20)
67.	Who will give their attention to prayer and the ministry of the word?
A.	The Twelve (6:4)
68.	For whom did these men wait at Troas?
A.	Paul and his companions (20:5)
69.	How did Paul go through Syria and Cilicia?
A.	Strengthening the churches (15:41)
70.	Who was staying with Simon the tanner, whose house was by the sea?
A.	Simon who was called Peter (10:6)
71.	Who called out, "Stand up on your feet!"?
A.	Paul (14:10)
72.	With what did King Herod have James, the brother of John, put to death?
A.	With the sword (12:2)
73.	According to Acts chapter 11: verse 20, where did some of them go?
A.	To Antioch (11:20)
74.	Who said, "People of Athens! I see that in every way you are very religious."?
A.	Paul (17:22)
75.	Who was also called Mark?
A.	John (12:12)
76.	According to Acts chapter 22: verse 17, who fell into a trance?
A.	Paul (22:17)
77.	Where did the son of Paul’s sister go?
A.	Into the barracks (23:16)
78.	In whom had the jailer and his whole household come to believe?
A.	God (16:34)
79.	Who made the people prosper during their stay in Egypt?
A.	The God of the people of Israel (13:17)
80.	For how long did they all shout in unison: "Great is Artemis of the Ephesians!"?
A.	About two hours (19:34)
81.	According to Acts chapter 9: verse 34, what did Aeneas do immediately?
A.	Got up (9:34)
82.	Whose daughter took Moses and brought him up as her own son?
A.	Pharaoh’s (7:21)
83.	To whom did King Agrippa and Bernice arrive at Caesarea a few days later to pay their respects?
A.	Festus (25:13)
84.	What was called Malta?
A.	The island (28:1)
85.	Who all wept as they embraced and kissed Paul?
A.	The elders of the church (20:37)
86.	From where did the rulers, the elders and the teachers of the law order Peter and John to withdraw?
A.	From the Sanhedrin (4:15)
87.	According to Acts chapter 7: verse 59, who prayed?
A.	Stephen (7:59)
88.	Who would not be dissuaded?
A.	Paul (21:14)
89.	What did some who made fun of the apostles say?
A.	"They have had too much wine." (2:13)
90.	Where did Paul and Barnabas spend considerable time?
A.	Iconium (14:3)
91.	Who saw Peter and John about to enter?
A.	A man who was lame from birth (3:3)
92.	How did Ananias himself violate the law?
A.	By commanding that Paul be struck (23:3)
93.	What did the wind not allow Paul and his companions to hold?
A.	Their course (27:7)
94.	Who appeared some time ago, claiming to be somebody?
A.	Theudas (5:36)
95.	Where has the law of Moses been preached from the earliest times?
A.	In every city (15:21)
96.	According to Acts chapter 13: verse 12, who saw what had happened?
A.	The proconsul (13:12)
97.	What had Abraham bought from the sons of Hamor at Shechem for a certain sum of money?
A.	The tomb (7:16)
98.	Before whom did Paul consider himself fortunate to stand?
A.	King Agrippa (26:2)
99.	According to Acts chapter 18: verse 1, where did Paul leave?
A.	Athens (18:1)
100.	What did the new believers in Samaria receive?
A.	The Holy Spirit (8:17)

A.	Paul (22:27)

A.	For the Spirit has sent them (10:20)

A.	Saul (9:2)

A.	When they heard this (19:28)

A.	Paul (24:21)

191.	What has never entered Peter’s mouth?

A.	Paul (20:18)

194.	Who wrote a letter?

200.	Who buried Stephen?
A.	Godly men (8:2)
Start of set
Set #2 Toss-ups

1.	Where did Paul meet a Jew named Aquila?
A.	In Corinth (18:2)
2.	Whom did Paul and his companions join at Troas five days later?
A.	The others (20:6)
3.	What did the centurion keep the soldiers from carrying out?
A.	Their plan (27:43)
4.	Where did Paul come about noon?
A.	Near Damascus (22:6)
5.	Who has received from the Father the promised Holy Spirit?
A.	This Jesus (2:33)
6.	Who spoke in tongues and prophesied?
A.	The disciples at Ephesus (19:6)
7.	Who said, "Look at us!"?
A.	Peter (3:4)
8.	According to Acts chapter 25: verse 10, where was Paul standing?
A.	Before Caesar’s court (25:10)
9.	Who buried Ananias?
A.	Some young men (5:6)
10.	Who will destroy this place and change the customs Moses handed down to us?
A.	Jesus of Nazareth (6:14)
11.	For what did Abraham buy the tomb from the sons of Hamor?
A.	A certain sum of money (7:16)
12.	Where did those who had been scattered preach the word?
A.	Wherever they went (8:4)
13.	What did Saul not eat or drink for three days?
A.	Anything (9:9)
14.	Before whom had some Jews agreed to ask the commander to bring Paul?
A.	The Sanhedrin (23:20)
15.	What was Peter still speaking?
A.	These words (10:44)
16.	Where did Herod and Pontius Pilate meet together with the Gentiles and the people of Israel?
A.	In this city (4:27)
17.	Who will not let his holy one see decay?
A.	God (13:35)
18.	Who knew the way Paul had lived ever since he was a child, from the beginning of his life in his own country, and also in Jerusalem?
A.	All the Jewish people (26:4)
19.	Who had gathered at the river?
A.	The women (16:13)
20.	Who criticized Peter?
A.	The circumcised believers (11:2)
21.	Who were very religious in every way?
A.	The people of Athens (17:22)
22.	Of whom was Philip one?
A.	The Seven (21:8)
23.	Who reported all that God had done through them and how he had opened a door of faith to the Gentiles?
A.	Paul and Barnabas (14:27)
24.	In what has the law of Moses been preached from the earliest times?
A.	Every city (15:21)
25.	Who expected Paul to swell up or suddenly fall dead?
A.	The people (28:6)
26.	Who ordered the centurion to keep Paul under guard but to give him some freedom and permit his friends to take care of his needs?
A.	Felix (24:23)
27.	Whom did many people who had gathered to pray see when they opened the door?
A.	Peter (12:16)
28.	Whose heart does the Lord know?
A.	Everyone’s (1:24)
29.	According to Acts chapter 5: verse 40, whom did they call in?
A.	The apostles (5:40)
30.	When did all the prison doors fly open?
A.	At once (16:26)
31.	Who saw Jesus standing at the right hand of God?
A.	Stephen (7:55)
32.	Who dismissed the young man?
A.	The commander (23:22)
33.	What had God’s power and will decided beforehand?
A.	What should happen (4:28)
34.	Where will God fill David with joy?
A.	In his presence (2:28)
35.	In what was the whole city of Jerusalem?
A.	An uproar (21:31)
36.	What has been sent to the children of Abraham, and you God-fearing Gentiles?
A.	This message of salvation (13:26)
37.	For what might Paul’s friends provide?
A.	His needs (27:3)
38.	Whom did a man named Simon amaze?
A.	All the people of Samaria (8:9)
39.	When was Paul on the road?
A.	About noon (26:13)
40.	Who stayed at Berea?
A.	Silas and Timothy (17:14)
41.	Through what did Saul’s followers lower him in a basket?
A.	Through an opening in the wall (9:25)
42.	In what did Felix leave Paul?
A.	Prison (24:27)
43.	Who said, "Stand up, I am only a man myself."?
A.	Peter (10:26)
44.	With whom did Paul stay and work?
A.	Aquila and Priscilla (18:3)
45.	What left them?
A.	Evil spirits (19:12)
46.	Where did the elders of the church accompany Paul?
A.	To the ship (20:38)
47.	Who said, "Silver or gold I do not have, but what I have I give you. In the name of Jesus Christ of Nazareth, walk."?
A.	Peter (3:6)
48.	What did the rest of the sick on the island do when this had happened?
A.	Came and were cured (28:9)
49.	When did God give them judges?
A.	After this (13:20)
50.	Bringing what did a famine strike all Egypt and Canaan?
A.	Great suffering (7:11)
51.	Who had never eaten anything impure or unclean?
A.	Peter (10:14)
52.	What are in agreement with this?
A.	The words of the prophets (15:15)
53.	What have four men with us made?
A.	A vow (21:23)
54.	Who told Aaron, "Make us gods who will go before us. As for this fellow Moses who led us out of Egypt—we don’t know what has happened to him!"?
A.	Our ancestors (7:40)
55.	Who ordered the chief priests and all the members of the Sanhedrin to assemble?
A.	The commander (22:30)
56.	What might Festus have as a result of the investigation?
A.	Something to write (25:26)
57.	Who has set the times and dates by his own authority?
A.	The Father (1:7)
58.	According to Acts chapter 11: verse 25, where did Barnabas go?
A.	To Tarsus (to look for Saul) (11:25)
59.	Who was at Corinth?
A.	Apollos (19:1)
60.	Who came to the border of Mysia?
A.	Paul and his companions (16:7)
61.	In what did Judas the Galilean appear?
A.	In the days of the census (5:37)

Set #26 Toss-ups

1.	In what was Simon who was called Peter a guest?
A.	In the home of Simon the tanner (who lived by the sea) (10:32)
2.	Who was just as zealous for God as any of you are today?
A.	Paul (22:3)
3.	How did the Spirit of the Lord take Philip away?
A.	Suddenly (8:39)
4.	What did Ananias himself violate?
A.	The law (23:3)
5.	Through what did God speak by the Holy Spirit?
A.	The mouth of his servant, our father David (4:25)
6.	According to Acts chapter 20: verse 31, what should you be?
A.	On your guard (20:31)
7.	What was there a conspiracy among the Jews to do?
A.	To kill Saul (9:23)
8.	According to Acts chapter 13: verse 51, where did Paul and Barnabas go?
A.	Iconium (13:51)
9.	Who came upon two Israelites who were fighting?
A.	Moses (7:26)
10.	Who was not insane?
A.	Paul (26:25)
11.	Who stood before the Sanhedrin?
A.	Paul (24:20)
12.	Who learned that Paul was preaching the word of God at Berea?
A.	The Jews in Thessalonica (17:13)
13.	Through what would the man and all his household be saved?
A.	The message (11:14)
14.	To whom did the disciples present these men?
A.	The apostles (6:6)
15.	What can they press?
A.	Charges (19:38)
16.	Who continued to preach the gospel?
A.	Paul and Barnabas (14:7)
17.	Who followed the advice of the pilot and of the owner of the ship?
A.	The centurion (27:11)
18.	Who devoted themselves to the apostle’s teaching and to fellowship, to the breaking of bread and to prayer?
A.	The people [OR the three thousand that were added to the apostle’s number] (2:42)
19.	Whose shadow might fall on some of the sick as he passed by?
A.	Peter’s (5:15)
20.	Who said to Peter, "Put on your clothes and sandals."?
A.	The angel (12:8)
21.	According to Acts chapter 15: verse 7, who addressed them?
A.	Peter (15:7)
22.	On what did a viper fasten itself?
A.	Paul’s hand (28:3)
23.	Who will be baptized with the Holy Spirit, in a few days?
A.	The apostles (1:5)
24.	When did Paul and his companions get ready at once to leave for Macedonia?
A.	After Paul had seen the vision (16:10)
25.	Whom did some Jews from the province of Asia stir up?
A.	The whole crowd (21:27)
26.	When did the chief priests and the elders of the Jews bring charges against Paul and ask that he be condemned?
A.	When Festus went to Jerusalem (25:15)
27.	Where did the Lord have many people?
A.	In that city (Corinth) (18:10)
28.	When were they still being driven across the Adriatic Sea?
A.	On the fourteenth night (27:27)
29.	By what must we help the weak?
A.	This kind of hard work (20:35)
30.	Who trembled with fear?
A.	Moses (7:32)
31.	From where did a sound like the blowing of a violent wind come?
A.	Heaven (2:2)
32.	Who was full of bitterness and captive to sin?
A.	Simon (8:23)
33.	Who were being called to account for an act of kindness shown to a man who was lame?
A.	Peter and John (4:9)
34.	What are in agreement with this?
A.	The words of the prophets (15:15)
35.	What spread through the whole region?
A.	The word of the Lord (13:49)
36.	For what did the lame man ask Peter and John?
A.	Money (3:3)
37.	When did the high priest and his associates call together the Sanhedrin—the full assembly of the elders of Israel?
A.	When they arrived (5:21)
38.	Who called Barnabas Zeus?
A.	The crowd (14:12)
39.	According to Acts chapter 16: verse 9, what did Paul have?
A.	A vision (16:9)
40.	Whom did Saul baffle by proving that Jesus is the Messiah?
A.	The Jews living in Damascus (9:22)
41.	What will God judge by the man he has appointed?
A.	The world (17:31)
42.	Who helped Paul had to this very day?
A.	God (26:22)
43.	Who went around doing good and healing all who were under the power of the devil?
A.	Jesus of Nazareth (10:38)
44.	Who remembered what the Lord had said?
A.	Peter (11:16)
45.	What was held in high honor?
A.	The name of the Lord Jesus (19:17)
46.	What has this man defiled?
A.	This holy place (21:28)
47.	Where would Paul be told all that he had been assigned to do?
A.	In Damascus (22:10)
48.	Who were convinced by what Paul said?
A.	Some (28:24)
49.	Who went over to get a closer look?
A.	Moses (7:31)
50.	How many times did this happen?
A.	Three (10:16)
51.	What does Elymas’ name mean?
A.	"The sorcerer" (13:8)
52.	Of whom did the believers at Lystra and Iconium speak well?
A.	Timothy (16:2)
53.	To whom did Claudius Lysias write a letter?
A.	His Excellency, Governor Felix (23:26)
54.	Who had James, the brother John, put to death with the sword?
A.	King Herod (12:2)
55.	According to Acts chapter 18: verse 19, whom did Paul leave?
A.	Priscilla and Aquila (18:19)
56.	Who would be able to learn the truth about all the charges the Jews were bringing against Paul by examining Paul himself?
A.	Felix [OR the governor] (24:8)
57.	From what was the Mount of Olives a Sabbath day’s walk?
A.	From the city (1:12)
58.	Who ordered Paul held until he could send him to Caesar?
A.	Festus (25:21)
59.	Who was a man accredited by God to you by miracles, wonders and signs?
A.	Jesus of Nazareth (2:22)
60.	What does God now command all people everywhere to do?
A.	Repent (17:30)
61.	Where did all the people rush?
A.	Into the theater (19:29)
62.	Whom did the disciples at Tyre urge not to go on to Jerusalem?
A.	Paul (21:4)
63.	Who has given the Holy Spirit to those who obey him?
A.	God (5:32)
64.	What were there among the believers?
A.	No needy persons (4:34)
65.	Where did Saul at once begin to preach that Jesus is the Son of God?
A.	In the synagogues (9:20)
66.	Where did our ancestors turn back to Egypt?
A.	In their hearts (7:39)
67.	Whom did the Israelites ask to be released to them?
A.	A murderer (3:14)
68.	Who said, "Give me also this ability so that everyone on whom I lay my hands may receive the Holy Spirit."?
A.	Simon (8:19)
69.	From where did a wind of hurricane force, called the Northeaster, sweep down?
A.	The island (27:14)
70.	To whom did the leaders of the synagogue send word?
A.	Paul and his companions (13:15)
71.	Whom have the Ephesians brought here?
A.	These men (19:37)
72.	Who was from Berea?
A.	Sopater son of Pyrrhus (20:4)
73.	Whom did Paul and Barnabas commit to the Lord with prayer and fasting?
A.	The elders (14:23)
74.	With whom did the apostles and elders, with the whole church, decide to send some of their own men to Antioch?
A.	Paul and Barnabas (15:22)
75.	Whom did the church in Jerusalem send to Antioch?
A.	Barnabas (11:22)
76.	What may your sins be?
A.	Wiped out (3:19)
77.	Whom did the captain and his officers fear would stone them?
A.	The people (5:26)
78.	Who spoke of the resurrection of the Messiah?
A.	David (2:31)
79.	By whom was Paul compelled to go to Jerusalem?
A.	The Spirit (20:22)
80.	According to Acts chapter 21: verse 1, where did they go the next day?
A.	Rhodes (21:1)
81.	To whom did Cornelius say, "Now we are all here in the presence of God to listen to everything the Lord has commanded you to tell us?"
A.	Peter (10:33)
82.	How did Paul say to the crowd, "Brothers and fathers, listen now to my defense."?
A.	In Aramaic (21:40-22:1)
83.	What had to do with questions about the Jews’ law?
A.	The accusation (23:29)
84.	Who were handed over to a centurion named Julius?
A.	Paul and some other prisoners (27:1)
85.	When did the believers take Saul down to Caesarea and send him off to Tarsus?
A.	When they learned of this (9:30)
86.	Where did Jacob and our ancestors die?
A.	In Egypt (7:15)
87.	From where did Gallio drive off the Jews of Corinth?
A.	The place of judgment (18:16)
88.	What is proclaimed to you through Jesus?
A.	The forgiveness of sins (13:38)
89.	Against whom did the Hellenistic Jews among them complain?
A.	The Hebraic Jews (6:1)
90.	Whom did Paul thank?
A.	God (28:15)
91.	According to Acts chapter 25: verse 8, what did Paul make?
A.	His defense (25:8)
92.	Between whom did God not discriminate?
A.	Jews and Gentiles (15:9)
93.	Where did Simon have such a thought?
A.	In his heart (8:22)
94.	To what did Lydia invite Paul and his companions?
A.	Her home (16:15)
95.	Where did the believers continue to meet together?
A.	In the temple courts (2:46)
96.	Who boarded a ship from Adramyttium about to sail for ports along the coast of the province of Asia?
A.	Paul and his companions (27:2)
97.	What did Stephen do among the people?
A.	Performed great wonders and signs (6:8)
98.	Who was on trial before the Sanhedrin?
A.	Paul (24:21)
99.	Whom does King Agrippa believe?
A.	The prophets (26:27)
100.	Whom had some Jews agreed to ask to bring Paul before the Sanhedrin?
A.	The commander (23:20)
101.	Who were ordered to withdraw from the Sanhedrin?
A.	Peter and John (4:15)
102.	Of whom is Jesus Christ Lord?
A.	All (10:36)
103.	What did the people read?
A.	The letter (15:31)
104.	Whom do you always resist?
A.	The Holy Spirit (7:51)
105.	When were the captain of the temple guard and the chief priests at a loss?
A.	On hearing this report (5:24)

A.	Paul and Silas [OR these men] (16:21)
107.	Where should the apostles not leave?
A.	Jerusalem (1:4)
108.	When did Paul and Barnabas report all that God had done through them and how he had opened a door of faith to the Gentiles?
A.	On arriving there (in Antioch) (14:27)
109.	Before whom did the mob drag Jason and some other believers?
A.	The city officials (17:6)
110.	On whom did Ananias place his hands?
A.	Saul (9:17)
111.	What did the crowds see?
A.	The signs Philip performed (8:6)
112.	What were the patriarchs?
A.	Jealous of Joseph (7:9)
113.	Who arrested some who belonged to the church, intending to persecute them?
A.	King Herod (12:1)
114.	Who must be received by Heaven until the time comes for God to restore everything?
A.	The Messiah (who has been appointed for you—even Jesus) (3:20-21)

A.	This man [OR Paul] (26:32)
116.	To what does Paul commit you?
A.	The word of God’s grace (20:32)
117.	In what must the Sanhedrin warn them to speak no longer to anyone?
A.	In this name (4:17)
118.	Where did they throw the grain?
A.	Into the sea (27:38)
119.	Who were glad and honored the word of the Lord?
A.	The Gentiles (13:48)
120.	Who said, "If you Jews were making a complaint about some misdemeanor or serious crime, it would be reasonable for me to listen to you."
A.	Gallio (18:14)
121.	What did some Jews who went around driving out evil spirits try to invoke?
A.	The name of the Lord Jesus (19:13)
122.	Who does not live in houses made by human hands?
A.	The Most High (7:48)
123.	When were some Jews ready to kill Paul?
A.	Before he got there (23:15)

A.	The prophet Joel (2:16)

A.	Paul and his companions (21:3)

A.	Saul (9:24)

A.	A man after God’s own heart (13:22)
129.	Whom were the chief priests and the Jewish leaders preparing an ambush to kill along the way?
A.	Paul (25:3)
130.	Why did Paul bring these people as prisoners to Jerusalem?
A.	To be punished (22:5)
131.	What came up the next day?
A.	The south wind (28:13)
132.	What is the God who made the world and everything in it?
A.	The Lord of heaven and earth (17:24)
133.	From where did the apostles never stop teaching and proclaiming the good news that Jesus is the Messiah?
A.	From house to house (5:42)
134.	How did Cornelius stare at the angel of God?
A.	In fear (10:4)
135.	What were some of the officials of the province?
A.	Friends of Paul (19:31)
136.	Who urged them to take some food?
A.	Paul (27:34)
137.	When did Joseph send for his father Jacob and his whole family?
A.	After this [OR after he told his brothers who he was] (7:13-14)
138.	Of what will Paul be God’s witness to all people?
A.	What he has seen and heard (22:15)
139.	Where did what seemed to be tongues of fire that separated come to rest?
A.	On each of them (2:3)
140.	In what could Peter not stand?
A.	God’s way (11:17)
141.	Who has fulfilled for us, their children, what he promised our fathers?
A.	God (13:32-33)
142.	What had brought about reforms in that nation?
A.	Felix’s foresight (24:2)
143.	What had Apollos been in the way of the Lord?
A.	Instructed (18:25)

A.	The people (21:30)

A.	Jesus (1:2)

A.	To the house of Judas on Straight Street (9:11)

A.	Abraham (7:4)
153.	Among whom was there no small commotion?
A.	The soldiers (12:18)
154.	Who proclaimed the kingdom of God?
A.	Paul (28:31)
155.	From what will men arise and distort the truth?
A.	Even from your own number (20:30)

159.	Whom did some of the Jews, a large number of God-fearing Greeks, and quite a few prominent women join?

A.	Himself (along with the men) (21:26)
168.	Who did not even know why they were there?
A.	Most of the people (19:32)

A.	If they could (27:39)

A.	Up to heaven (7:55)

A.	Rather than human beings (5:29)

A.	Charges (24:19)

A.	Speak his word with great boldness (4:29)

A.	God (7:3)

A.	Publicly and from house to house (20:20)

A.	A drachma (19:19)

Start of set
Set #27 Toss-ups

1.	Whose face was like the face of an angel?
A.	Stephen’s (6:15)
2.	Who presented his case before Felix?
A.	Tertullus (24:2)
3.	What is no ordinary city?
A.	Tarsus in Cilicia (21:39)
4.	Whom did many of the Jews and devout converts to Judaism follow?
A.	Paul and Barnabas (13:43)
5.	Who enabled them to speak in other tongues?
A.	The Spirit (2:4)
6.	Whose temple was just outside the city?
A.	The priest of Zeus’ (14:13)
7.	Where were the chief priests and the Jewish leaders preparing an ambush to kill Paul?
A.	Along the way (25:3)
8.	Into what did Paul fall?
A.	A trance (22:17)
9.	When were Paul and Silas praying and singing hymns to God?
A.	About midnight (16:25)
10.	With what is the king familiar?
A.	These things (26:26)
11.	In what did our ancestors revel?
A.	In what their own hands had made (7:41)
12.	Whom has God given to those who obey him?
A.	The Holy Spirit (5:32)
13.	Whom did the centurion take to the commander?
A.	The young man [OR the son of Paul’s sister] (23:18)
14.	Where did Barnabas go to look for Saul?
A.	Tarsus (11:25)
15.	Where must anything further be settled?
A.	In a legal assembly (19:39)
16.	How was the church throughout Judea, Galilee and Samaria encouraged?
A.	By the Holy Spirit (9:31)
17.	When did an angel of the God to whom Paul belongs whom he serves stand beside him?
A.	Last night (27:23)
18.	Who called out, asking if Simon who was known as Peter was staying there?
A.	The men sent by Cornelius (10:18)
19.	What did the people of Tyre and Sidon seek?
A.	An audience with Herod (12:20)
20.	To where did certain people come down from Judea?
A.	Antioch (15:1)
21.	When did the believers send Paul and Silas away to Berea?
A.	As soon as it was night (17:10)
22.	According to Acts chapter 18: verse 17, who was the synagogue leader?
A.	Sosthenes (18:17)
23.	From where were Aristarchus and Secundus?
A.	Thessalonica (20:4)
24.	What did Joseph bring?
A.	The money (4:37)
25.	With what did Simon think he could buy the gift of God?
A.	Money (8:20)
26.	To whom did Peter say, "Why do you stare at us as if by our own power or godliness we had made this man walk?"
A.	Fellow Israelites (3:12)
27.	When did the rest of the sick on the island come?
A.	When this had happened (28:9)
28.	Who spent several days with the disciples in Damascus?
A.	Saul (9:19)
29.	Who left Paul and his companions to return to Jerusalem?
A.	John (13:13)
30.	Who will send Moses back to Egypt?
A.	The Lord (7:34)
31.	According to Acts chapter 4: verse 23, who were released?
A.	Peter and John (4:23)
32.	Where did the Spirit tell Philip to go?
A.	To that chariot (8:29)
33.	What were the apostles and elders sending Judas and Silas to confirm by word of mouth?
A.	What they were writing (15:27)
34.	Whom will none of those among whom Paul has gone about preaching the kingdom ever see again?
A.	Paul (20:25)
35.	To whom did the man who was mistreating the other say, "Are you thinking of killing me as you killed the Egyptian yesterday?"
A.	Moses (7:28)
36.	Who appeared to the apostles over a period of forty days and spoke about the kingdom of God?
A.	Jesus (1:3)
37.	Who will dream dreams?
A.	Your old men (2:17)
38.	How did Ananias sit there to judge Paul?
A.	According to the law (23:3)
39.	How did God bless you?
A.	By sending his servant first to you [OR by turning each of you from your wicked ways] (3:26)
40.	When were they approaching the city?
A.	About noon the following day (10:9)
41.	According to Acts chapter 5: verse 36, who appeared?
A.	Theudas (5:36)
42.	What is the guardian of the temple of Artemis and her image?
A.	The city of Ephesus (19:35)
43.	Whom did the Egyptian lead out into the wilderness some time ago?
A.	Four thousand terrorists (21:38)
44.	Who believed and turned to the Lord?
A.	A great number of people (11:21)
45.	How did the churches grow in numbers?
A.	Daily (16:5)
46.	Until when did Festus order Paul held?
A.	Until he could send Paul to Caesar (25:21)
47.	What did they finally give up?
A.	All hope of being saved (27:20)
48.	Who commanded them to preach to the poor and to testify that he is the one whom God appointed as judge of the living and the dead?
A.	Jesus (of Nazareth) (10:42)
49.	On what did the people invite Paul and Barnabas to speak further about these things?
A.	The next Sabbath (13:42)
50.	What did all the people, both high and low, give Simon?
A.	Their attention (8:10)
51.	Who were members of the party of the Sadducees?
A.	The high priest and all his associates (5:17)
52.	Instead of what did the centurion follow the advice of the pilot and the owner of the ship?
A.	Listening to what Paul said (27:11)
53.	Whom did some of the Jews, a large number of God-fearing Greeks, and quite a few prominent women join?
A.	Paul and Silas (17:4)
54.	How did Paul and Barnabas go into the Jewish synagogue?
A.	As usual (14:1)
55.	Who said, "Men of Galilee, why do you stand here looking into the sky? This same Jesus, who has been taken from you into heaven, will come back in the same way you have seen him go into heaven."?
A.	Two men dressed in white (1:10-11)
56.	As what would the Messiah bring the message of light to his own people?
A.	The first to rise from the dead (26:23)
57.	Who reasoned in the synagogue every Sabbath, trying to persuade Jews and Greeks?
A.	Paul (18:4)
58.	For what did the commander have to pay a lot of money?
A.	His citizenship (22:28)
59.	What did Paul place on the disciples at Ephesus?
A.	His hands (19:6)

A.	One of the centurions (23:17)

A.	God and man (24:16)

A.	Through Syria and Cilicia (15:41)

A.	By throwing the grain into the sea (27:38)

A.	Greatly (7:17)

A.	The Council (17:33)

A.	Stephen (7:60)

A.	The disciples (11:29)

A.	Paul (20:27)

A.	In detail (21:19)

A.	At the sight of these people (28:15)

A.	Peter (12:11)

A.	Attalia (14:25)

A.	The sea (27:30)

A.	When he received these orders (16:24)

A.	Bedridden for eight years (9:33)

A.	Treacherously (7:19)

A.	Some of the men of Athens [OR some of the Epicurean and Stoic philosophers] (17:32)

A.	The Lord’s footstool (7:49)

199.	Who suddenly took Philip away?

200.	When did the apostles never stop teaching and proclaiming the good news that Jesus is the Messiah?
